本科专业培养计划
Undergraduate Program for Electronic Information Engineering Major
[2024级适用]
电子信息工程专业（080701）
大连海事大学教务处
2024年9月
电子信息工程专业本科培养计划
Undergraduate Program for Electronic Information Engineering Major
一、专业简介
I．Program Profile
电子信息工程专业前身是始建于1958年的船舶电气与导航专业，1960年更名为船舶无线电导航专业，1984年更名为电子工程专业，1989年更名为电子信息工程专业。本专业面向现代海洋经济电子信息领域国家重大战略和经济发展需求，以立德树人为本，培养政治立场坚定，具有良好综合素养，能够结合人工智能新一代信息技术在无线电导航、雷达、海上通信相关领域从事科学研究、设计开发、测试运维和服务管理等工作的专业技术人才和行业骨干。50多年来为国家和涉海行业、企业培养了近万名的专业技术和管理人才。
本专业为国家级一流本科专业建设点，依托大连海事大学信息与通信工程一级重点学科，是国家优势特色专业、交通运输部重点建设专业、辽宁省优势特色专业、辽宁省一流本科示范专业、辽宁省综合改革示范专业、辽宁省创新创业教育改革试点专业、学校211重点建设专业，2013年辽宁省专业排名第一。专业坚持“宽口径、厚基础、实践与创新并举”的人才培养模式，培育具备电子信息技术、海上通信导航技术和人工智能技术知识和创新应用能力的综合型人才，服务于国家“海洋强国”和“交通强国”战略。
本专业的毕业生主要从事IT领域相关通信、导航、雷达等电子信息系统和设备生产企业及研究单位的技术研发，港航企业和海事管理部门等的技术管理,以及从事通信导航等信息系统工程设计单位的工程设计等。
The precursor of the major of Electronic Information Engineering was established in 1958 as the Marine Electrical and Navigation Engineering major. It was renamed as Marine Radio Navigation major in 1960, and became the Electronic Engineering major in 1984. It was finally renamed as Electronic Information Engineering major in 1989. This major is geared towards the national strategic needs and economic development requirements of the modern maritime electronic information field. It is rooted in cultivating individuals with strong political stances and good overall quality, capable of engaging in scientific research, design and developing, testing and operation, and service management in the fields of radio navigation, radar, and maritime communication, integrating the new generation of artificial intelligence technologies. Over the past 50 years, it has cultivated nearly ten thousand professional and managerial talents for the nation, maritime industries, and enterprises.
The major is recognized as a national first-class undergraduate program construction point, relying on the first-level key discipline of Information and Communication Engineering at Dalian Maritime University. It is a national advantageous characteristic major, a key construction major of the Ministry of Transport, an advantageous characteristic major of Liaoning Province, a first-class undergraduate demonstration major of Liaoning Province, a comprehensive reform demonstration major of Liaoning Province, an innovation and entrepreneurship education reform pilot major of Liaoning Province, and a key construction major of Dalian Maritime University under the 211 Project. In 2013, it ranked first among
majors in Liaoning Province. The major adheres to the talent cultivation model of "broad caliber, solid foundation, practice and innovation combined", nurturing comprehensive talents with knowledge and innovative application capabilities in electronic information technology, maritime communication and navigation technology, and artificial intelligence technology, serving the national strategies of "Maritime Power" and "Transportation Power".
Graduates of this major mainly engage in technical research and development in equipment production enterprises and research institutions of electronic information systems related to the IT field, such as communication, navigation, radar, etc., technical management in port and maritime management departments, as well as engineering design in the communication and navigation information system.
二、培养目标
II．Program Objectives
本专业贯彻落实党的教育方针，坚持立德树人，服务“海洋强国”和“交通强国”战略，培养具有较扎实的自然科学基础知识和专业理论技术知识，具备良好的人文社会科学综合素养，能够在电子信息工程相关领域从事科学研究、设计开发、测试运维和服务管理等工作的专业技术人才及行业骨干。
五年以上本专业毕业生应具备：
（1）能够综合运用工程知识解决电子信息相关领域的复杂工程问题，在工程问题解决过程中体现创新意识，并综合考虑社会、环境、法规、健康、安全与文化等因素影响；
（2）在职业生涯中具有良好的人文社会科学素养、社会责任感和职业道德；
（3）具备国际视野，具有沟通、交流与管理能力，在工作团队中，能作为主要成员发挥骨干作用；
（4）具有自主学习和适应发展能力，具备终身学习意识。
This major implements the educational policies of Communist Party of China, adheres to the principle of moral education and talent cultivation, and serves the national strategies of "Maritime Power" and "Transportation Power". It aims to cultivate professional and technical talents and industry leaders who have a solid foundation in natural sciences and professional theoretical knowledge, possess good comprehensive literacy in humanities and social sciences, and are capable of engaging in scientific research, design and developing, testing and operation, and service management in the field of electronic information engineering.
Graduates over five years should have the abilities:
Using engineering knowledge to solve complex engineering problems in electronic information field, with considering social, environmental, regulatory, health, safety and cultural factors, and with innovative consciousness in the process of solving engineering problems.
With good humanities and Social Sciences literacy, social responsibility and professional ethics in their career;
Having international vision, communication and management skills, and being able to play a backbone role as a key member in a team.
Having the ability to learn independently and adapt to the development of society, and having the consciousness of lifelong learning.
三、毕业要求
III．Graduation Requirements
本专业学生毕业时应掌握和具备以下几方面的知识与能力：
Our Graduate Attribute Profile has 12 elements, supported by a Knowledge Profile and a definition of the Level of Problem Solving, both given below:
1、工程知识：能够将数学和自然科学基础知识，工程基础知识，电子电路、信号与系统等专业基础知识和电子信息工程专业知识，用于解决电子信息相关领域复杂工程问题。
1.Engineering knowledge: Utilize the knowledge of mathematics and natural science, engineering, electronic circuit, signal and system, electronic information engineering etc. to solve complex engineering problems in the field of electronic information.
2、问题分析：能够应用工程知识基本原理，对电子信息工程相关领域复杂工程问题进行识别和表达，并通过文献研究分析这些问题，从而获得有效结论。
2.Problem analysis: Identify and describe complex engineering problems of electronic information engineering utilizing the basic principles of Engineering knowledge, analyze these problems through literature research, and obtain the effective conclusions.
3、设计/开发解决方案：能够针对电子信息工程相关领域复杂工程问题，进行特定需求分析，在考虑社会、健康、安全、法律、文化以及环境等因素基础上，设计相应复杂工程问题的解决方案，并在设计中体现创新意识。
3.Design/development of solutions: Analyze the specific requirement of complex engineering problems of electronic information engineering, design or develop solutions to these complex engineering problems with considering social, health, safety, law, culture and environment factors, and with innovative consciousness in the design.
4、研究：能够基于科学原理并采用科学方法对电子信息工程相关领域复杂工程问题进行研究，设计实验方案，分析和解释实验/试验数据，并通过综合研究结果和实验/试验数据等信息得到合理有效的结论。
4.Investigation: Research complex engineering problems of electronic information engineering with scientific principles and scientific methods, design experimental schemes, analyze and interpret experimental/experimental data, and obtain reasonable and effective conclusions by synthesizing research results and experimental/experimental data.
5、使用现代工具：能够开发、选择与使用适当的技术、资源、现代工程工具和信息技术工具，对电子信息工程相关领域复杂工程问题进行预测与模拟; 采集、整理和使用复杂工程问题相关信息数据；在现代工具使用过程中，理解其局限性。
5. Modern tool usage: Develop, select and use appropriate technology, resources, modern engineering tools and information technology tools, to predict and simulate complex engineering problems of electronic information engineering; collect, process and utilize the information data which is related to those complex engineering problems, and understand their limitations of modern tools.
6、工程与社会：能够基于相关工程背景知识，分析和评价电子信息领域相关工程实践和复杂工程问题解决方案对社会、健康、安全、法律以及文化的影响，并理解应承担责任。
6. The engineer and society: Analyze and evaluate the influence of the social, health, safety, legal and cultural on the engineering practices of electronic information engineering and the solutions of their complex engineering problems with consideration of their engineering background, and understand relevant responsibilities.
7、环境与可持续发展：能够理解和评价在解决电子信息工程领域相关复杂工程问题中，工程实践对环境、社会可持续发展的影响。
7. Environment and sustainability: Understand and evaluate the engineering practices impact on the sustainable development of the environment and society in solving complex engineering problems of electronic information engineering.
8、职业规范：具有人文社会科学素养和社会责任感，能够在电子信息工程实践中理解并遵守工程职业道德规范，履行责任。
8. Ethics: Have humanities and social sciences literacy, and social responsibility, understand and abide by engineering professional ethics in electronic information engineering practice, and fulfill their responsibilities.
9、个人和团队：能够在多学科背景下的团队中承担个体、团队成员以及负责人的角色。
9. Individual and teamwork: Work effectively as an individual, a member or leader in a diverse teams and in multi-disciplinary settings.
10、沟通：能够就电子信息工程相关领域复杂工程问题与业界同行及社会公众进行有效沟通和交流，包括撰写报告和设计文稿、陈述发言、清晰表达或回应指令。并具备一定的国际视野，能够在跨文化背景下进行沟通和交流。
10. Communication: Communicate effectively with industry counterparts, the public people on the complex engineering issues of electronic information engineering, including writing reports, designing documentation, presenting statements, clearly expressing or responding to instructions. And have a certain international perspective, communicate in cross-cultural context.
11、项目管理：理解并掌握工程管理原理与经济决策方法，并能在多学科环境中应用。
11 .Project management and finance: Understand and master engineering management principles and economic decision-making methods, and apply them in a multidisciplinary environment.
12、终身学习：具有自主学习和终身学习的意识，有不断学习以适应发展的能力。
12. Life-long learning: Have the consciousness of self-learning and lifelong learning, have the ability of continuous learning to adapt to the development.
四、特色课程
IV．Feature Courses
导航原理与设备、导航信息处理、雷达原理与设备、船舶交通管理电子信息系统、导航接收机技术、信号检测与处理、空间信息技术基础。
Navigation Principles and Equipment, Navigation information process, RADAR Principles and Equipment, Electronic Information System for Vessel Traffic Services, Navigation Receiver Technology, Signal Detecting and Processing, Space Information Technology.
五、学制与学位
V．Duration and Degree
学制：4年
Program Duration：4 years
授予学位：工学学士学位
Degree conferred：Bachelor of Engineering

后    记
培养计划是高等学校人才培养的纲领性文件，是教育思想和办学理念的集中体现，是实现人才培养目标的具体实施方案。根据学校质量体系文件《培养计划的制定与修订》（DMU-2-040）的要求，本年度培养计划在2021年修订版基础上做了微调。在多次校对、反复审核的过程当中，得到了各教学单位领导、教务、以及老师的大力支持和帮助。在此，对在培养计划修订过程中给予支持和帮助的各位，表示衷心的感谢。
培养计划的制定是一项繁琐的系统工作，难免会有疏漏，不足之处还望批评指正。培养计划的修订是以专业发展和知识更新为需求导向的，在执行过程中会进行细微调整。在此过程中，若产生分歧，应以教务系统为准。

本科专业培养计划
Undergraduate Program for
Electronic Information Science and Technology Major
[2024级适用]
电子信息科学与技术（080714T）
大连海事大学教务处
2024年9月
电子信息科学与技术专业本科培养计划
Undergraduate Program for Electronic Information Science and Technology Major
一、专业简介
I．Program Profile
电子信息科学与技术专业1998年列入教育部公布的高等学校招生专业目录，是一个跨学科、厚基础、宽口径、实用性强、服务面广的专业，涵盖了电子科学技术和信息技术两个领域。我校该专业从2001年开始招生，2008年被评为辽宁省普通高等学校本科示范专业，2013年被评为辽宁省普通高等学校本科工程人才培养模式改革试点专业，2019年入选一流本科专业建设“双万计划”辽宁省普通高等学校一流本科教育示范专业。
本专业分为基于计算机视觉与语音、射频通信与网络、集成电路与微电子器件三个方向。
本专业是我校信息与通信工程一级学科博士点和一级学科硕士点的主要支撑专业之一。
本专业学生入学后可申请我校与休斯顿大学电子工程专业、爱尔兰国立梅努斯大学、法国图尔弗朗索瓦·拉伯雷大学工程学院和法国奥尔良大学等国际大学的合作办学项目。
Electronic information science and technology major was released by Ministry of Education as college admissions professional directory in 1998. It is an interdisciplinary, practical and wide-ranged major that covers both electronic science and technology and information technology areas. DMU starts its enrollment for this major in the beginning of 2001. And this major was assessed as “Liaoning Province Demonstration Major for Higher Education Undergraduates” in 2008 and it was built as “Liaoning Province Undergraduate Engineering Talent Training Pilot Project” in 2013. This program is divided into three concentration areas, which are computer vision and speech signal, radio frequency communication and network, and integrated circuits and microelectronic devices.
After enrollment, students of this major can apply for the cooperative projects of DMU with some international universities such as Houston University, Ireland National Menus University, Tourfrancois Rabelais University College of Engineering and the University of Orleans in France.
二、培养目标
II．Program Objectives
本专业旨在培养适应社会与信息技术发展需求，具有良好的社会责任感、职业道德、人文素养、科学素养和家国情怀，具有国际视野、跨文化交流能力和创新能力，系统掌握电子信息领域的基础理论和专业知识，具备良好的终身学习能力，能够在电子信息科学与技术相关领域从事科学研究、设计开发、测试运维和服务管理等工作的高素质工程技术人才与德智体美劳全面发展的社会主义建设者和接班人。
本专业学生毕业五年左右应具有以下职业能力：
（1）能够综合运用工程知识解决电子信息科学与技术领域的工程问题，在工程问题解决过程中体现创新意识，并综合考虑社会、环境、法规、健康、安全与文化等因素影响；
（2）在职业生涯中具有良好的人文社会科学素养、社会责任感和职业道德；
（3）具有国际视野，沟通、交流与管理能力，在工作团队中，能作为主要成员发挥骨干作用；
（4）具有自主学习和适应发展能力，具备终身学习意识。
The program aims to cultivate high-quality engineering technical talents, socialist builders and successors with all-round development in morality, intelligence, physique, aesthetics and labor, who can adapt to the development needs of society and information technology, have a good sense of social responsibility, professional ethics, humanistic literacy, scientific literacy and patriotism, possess international vision, cross-cultural communication ability and innovation ability, systematically grasp the basic theories and professional knowledge in the field of electronic information, and have good lifelong learning ability. They are able to engage in scientific research, design and development, testing, operation and maintenance, service management and other work in related fields of electronic information science and technology.
Graduates of this program should have the following professional abilities in about five years after graduation:
They can identify, formulate, and solve complex electrical engineering related problems by applying principles of engineering, science, and mathematics with consideration of public health, safety, and welfare, as well as global, cultural, social, environmental, and economic factors;
They will possess good humanities and social sciences literacy, social responsibility and professional ethics in their career;
They will have international vision, communication and management skills, and being able to play a backbone role as a key member in a team;
They will have the ability to learn independently and adapt to the development of society, and having the consciousness of lifelong learning, engage in self-development activities that will allow them to adapt to evolving technical challenges and changing career opportunities.
三、毕业要求
III. Graduation requirements
本专业学生毕业时应掌握和具备以下12方面的知识与能力：
Our Graduate Attribute Profile has 12 elements, supported by a Knowledge Profile and a definition of the Level of Problem Solving, both given below:
1.工程知识：能够将数学和自然科学基础知识，工程基础知识，电子电路、信号与系统等专业基础知识和电子信息科学与技术领域专业知识，用于解决电子信息科学与技术领域复杂工程问题。
1.Engineering knowledge: Utilize the knowledge of mathematics and natural science, engineering, electronic circuit, signal and system, etc. to solve complex engineering problems in the field of electronic information technology.
2.问题分析：能够应用工程知识基本原理，对电子信息科学与技术领域复杂工程问题进行识别和表达，并通过文献研究分析这些问题，从而获得有效结论。
2.Problem analysis: Identify and describe complex engineering problems in the field of electronic information technology，utilizing the basic principles of Engineering knowledge, analyze these problems through literature research, and obtain the effective conclusions.
3.设计/开发解决方案：能够针对电子信息科学与技术领域复杂工程问题，进行特定需求分析，在考虑社会、健康、安全、法律、文化以及环境等因素基础上，设计相应复杂工程问题的解决方案，并在设计中体现创新意识。
3. Design/development of solutions: Analyze the specific requirement of complex engineering problems in the field of electronic information technology, design or develop solutions to these complex engineering problems with considering social, health, safety, law, culture and environment factors, and with innovative consciousness in the design.
4.研究：能够基于科学原理并采用科学方法对电子信息科学与技术领域复杂工程问题进行研究，设计实验方案，分析和解释实验/试验数据，并通过综合研究结果和实验/试验数据等信息得到合理有效的结论。
4. Investigation: Research complex engineering problems in the field of electronic information technology with scientific principles and scientific methods, design experimental schemes, analyze and interpret experimental/experimental data, and obtain reasonable and effective conclusions by synthesizing research results and experimental/experimental data.
5.使用现代工具：能够开发、选择与使用适当的技术、资源、现代工程工具和信息技术工具，对电子信息科学与技术领域复杂工程问题进行预测与模拟;采集、整理和使用复杂工程问题相关信息数据；在现代工具使用过程中，理解其局限性。
5. Modern tool usage: Develop, select and use appropriate technology, resources, modern engineering tools and information technology tools, to predict and simulate complex engineering problems in the field of electronic information technology; collect, process and utilize the information data which is related to those complex engineering problems, and understand their limitations of modern tools.
6.工程与社会：能够基于电子信息科学与技术领域相关工程背景知识，分析和评价电子信息科学与技术领域工程实践和复杂工程问题解决方案对社会、健康、安全、法律以及文化的影响，并理解应承担责任。
6. The engineering and society: Analyze and evaluate the influence of the social, health, safety, legal and cultural on the engineering practices in the field of electronic information technology and the solutions of their complex engineering problems with consideration of their engineering background, and understand relevant responsibilities.
7.环境与可持续发展：能够理解和评价在解决电子信息科学与技术领域复杂工程问题中，工程实践对环境、社会可持续发展的影响。
7. Environment and sustainability: Understand and evaluate the engineering practices impact on the sustainable development of the environment and society in solving complex engineering problems in the field of electronic information technology.
8.职业规范：具有人文社会科学素养和社会责任感，能够在电子信息科学与技术领域工程实践中理解并遵守工程职业道德规范，履行责任。
8. Ethics: Have humanities and social sciences literacy, and social responsibility, understand and abide by engineering professional ethics in the engineering project in field of electronic information technology, and fulfill their responsibilities.
9.个人和团队：能够在多学科背景下的团队中承担个体、团队成员以及负责人的角色。
9. Individual and teamwork: Work effectively as an individual, a member or leader in a diverse team and in multi-disciplinary settings.
10、沟通：能够就电子信息科学与技术领域复杂工程问题与业界同行及社会公众进行有效沟通和交流，包括撰写报告和设计文稿、陈述发言、清晰表达或回应指令。并具备一定的国际视野，能够在跨文化背景下进行沟通和交流。
10. Communication: Communicate effectively with industry counterparts, the public people on the complex engineering issues in the field of electronic information technology, including writing reports, designing documentation, presenting statements, clearly expressing or responding to instructions. And have a certain international perspective, communicate in cross-cultural context.
11.项目管理：理解并掌握工程管理原理与经济决策方法，并能在多学科环境中应用。
11. Project management and finance: Understand and master engineering management principles and economic decision-making methods, and apply them in a multidisciplinary environment.
12.终身学习：具有自主学习和终身学习的意识，有不断学习以适应发展的能力。
12. Life-long learning: Have the consciousness of self-learning and lifelong learning, have the ability of continuous learning to adapt to the development.
四、特色课程
IV．Feature Courses
数字图像处理、机器视觉系统、图像压缩技术、智能视觉与深度学习、语音信号处理；微电子技术基础、微电子器件、FPGA数字系统设计、SOPC技术；微波技术、电波与天线、射频电路设计、数字微波通信；嵌入式系统、统计信号处理、Python编程与机器学习基础。
Digital Image Processing, Machine Vision System, Image Compression Technology, Visual Intelligence and Deep Learning, Speech Signal Processing; Introduction of Microelectronics, Microelectronic Device, Digital System Design with FPGA, SOPC Technology; Microwave Technology, Radio Wave Propagation and Antennas, Fundamentals of RF Circuits Design, Digital Microwave Communication; Design of Embedded System, Statistical Signal Processing, Introduction to Python Programming & Machine Learning.

学制：4年

后    记
培养计划是高等学校人才培养的纲领性文件，是教育思想和办学理念的集中体现，是实现人才培养目标的具体实施方案。根据学校质量体系文件《培养计划的制定与修订》（DMU-2-040）的要求，本年度培养计划在2021年修订版基础上做了微调。在多次校对、反复审核的过程当中，得到了各教学单位领导、教务、以及老师的大力支持和帮助。在此，对在培养计划修订过程中给予支持和帮助的各位，表示衷心的感谢。
培养计划的制定是一项繁琐的系统工作，难免会有疏漏，不足之处还望批评指正。培养计划的修订是以专业发展和知识更新为需求导向的，在执行过程中会进行细微调整。在此过程中，若产生分歧，应以教务系统为准。

本科专业培养计划
Undergraduate Program for
Marine Electrical and Electronic Engineering Major
[2024级适用]
光电信息科学与工程（080705）
大连海事大学教务处
2024年9月
光电信息科学与工程专业本科培养计划
Undergraduate Program for Opto-Electronics Information Science and Engineering Major
一、专业简介
I．Program Profile
光电信息科学与工程专业是一个新兴、复合型专业，涉及光电技术、计算机、电子学、信息技术、图像处理、通信等诸多学科的理论知识和方法应用。具有多学科、综合性、工程性、应用广泛性等特点。大连海事大学光电信息科学与工程专业的前身是成立于2006年并于2010开始招收本科生的光电信息工程专业，于2013年教育部统一更名为光电信息科学与工程专业。
Optoelectronic Information Science and Engineering is a new and complex program that covers the Theory of Optoelectronic Technology, Computer, Electronics, Information Technology, Image Processing, Communication and other theoretical knowledge and methods from various disciplines. Focusing on its multi-disciplinary, comprehensive, engineering and universal characteristics, this program was firstly established in 2006, and it was renamed as Optoelectronic Information Science and Engineering in 2013 by Ministry of Education.
二、培养目标
II．Program Objectives
本专业培养适应社会主义现代化建设需求，具备光电信息科学与工程基本理论、基本知识和基本技能，掌握光电信息工程的理论、应用和最新发展动态，能在光电信息工程及相关的电子信息工程、计算机工程等领域从事技术研发、产品设计、科学研究、教学与管理等工作的德、智、体全面发展的高级专业技术人才。
This program aims to develop the students’ ability to meet the needs of socialist modernization, possessing the basic skills that cover basic theories, knowledge and skills of Optoelectronic Information Science and Engineering. With the knowledge of the theory, application and latest trends of optoelectronic information engineering, related electronic information engineering and computer engineering, students will engage in the field of technology development, product design, scientific research, education and management as compound talents.
三、毕业要求
III. Graduation requirements
本专业学生毕业时应掌握和具备以下几方面的知识与能力：
Our Graduate Attribute Profile has 12 elements, supported by a Knowledge Profile and a definition of the Level of Problem Solving, both given below:
1、工程知识：能够将数学、自然科学、工程基础理论和专业知识用于解决光电信息科学与工程领域中的复杂工程问题；
1.Engineering knowledge: Apply knowledge of material science based mathematics, natural science, engineering fundamentals and an engineering specialization respectively to the solution of complex engineering problems;
2、问题分析：能够应用数学、自然科学和光电信息科学的基本原理，识别、表达并通过文献研究分析光电信息领域的复杂工程问题；
2.Problem analysis: Identify, formulate, describe and analyze complex engineering problems reaching substantiated conclusions using first principles of mathematics, natural sciences and material sciences;
3、设计/开发解决方案：能够进行光电信息系统的采集、传输、处理、存储以及显示利用的全周期和全流程设计，或为满足特定需求的光电设备或工艺流程进行设计以解决复杂工程问题，并在设计环节中体现出创新意识，考虑社会、健康、安全、法律、文化、环境等问题；
3.Design/development of solutions: Design solutions for complex engineering problems and design new materials, technology, components or processes that meet specified needs with appropriate consideration for public health, and safety, cultural, societal and environmental considerations;
4、研究：能够基于光电信息科学原理并采用科学的方法通过设计、实施实验方案、分析、解释实验结果与数据对复杂的光电信息科学与工程领域问题进行研究，并通过综合各方面的信息得出合理有效的结论；
4.Investigation: Conduct investigations of complex problems using fundamental knowledge of material science and research methods including design of experiments, analysis and interpretation of data, and synthesis of information to provide valid conclusions.
5、使用现代工具：能够针对光电信息领域复杂工程问题，开发、选择与使用适当的技术、资源、现代工程工具和信息技术工具，使用有效的方法进行理论和模拟分析并能够理解其适用范围；
5. Modern tool usage: Have the good knowledge on the techniques, resources and modern engineering and IT tools regarding to the material science, and create, select and apply appropriate items, including prediction and modeling, to complex engineering problems;
6、工程与社会：能够基于光电信息系统和设备研制过程有关的工程背景知识，分析和评价光电信息领域工程实践和复杂工程问题解决方案对社会、健康、安全、法律以及文化的影响，并理解应承担责任；
6. The engineer and society: Apply reasoning informed by materials knowledge to assess societal, health, safety, legal and cultural issues and the consequent responsibilities relevant to material engineering practice and solutions to complex engineering problems;
7、环境与可持续发展：能够理解和评价针对光电信息科学与工程领域复杂工程问题的工程实践对环境、社会可持续发展的影响；
7. Environment and sustainability: Understand and evaluate the sustainability and impact of engineering work in the solution of complex material engineering problems in societal and environmental contexts;
8、职业规范：爱国守法，具有人文社会科学素养和社会责任感，能够在光电信息科学与工程实施过程中理解并遵守工程职业道德规范，履行相应的责任；
8. Ethics: Apply ethical principles and commit to professional ethics and responsibilities and norms of materials engineering practice;
9、个人和团队：能够在多学科背景的团队中承担个体、团队成员以及负责人的角色，具备良好的团队合作精神、协调能力与责任意识；
9. Individual and teamwork: Function effectively as an individual, and as a member or leader in diverse teams and in multi-disciplinary settings;
10、沟通：能够就光电信息系统、设备的制造与研究中的复杂工程问题与业界同行及社会公众进行书面和口头的沟通和交流；并具备一定的国际视野，能够在跨文化背景下进行沟通和交流；
10. Communication: Communicate effectively on complex materials engineering problems with the engineering community and society at large, such as being able to comprehend and write effective reports and design documentation, make effective presentations and give and receive clear instructions.
11、项目管理：理解并掌握光电信息科学与技术相关的工程项目管理原理与经济决策方法，并能在解决光电信息科学与工程问题的多学科环境中应用；
11. Project management and finance: Demonstrate knowledge and understanding of material engineering management principles and economic decision-making and apply these to one’s own work as a member and leader in a team, to manage projects and in multi-disciplinary environments.
12、终身学习：具有自主学习和终身学习的意识，有不断学习和适应发展的能力。
12. Life-long learning: Recognize the need for, and have the preparation and ability to engage in, independent and life-long learning in the broadest context of technological change.
四、特色课程
IV．Feature Courses
EDA技术、光学系统设计、光电图像处理、嵌入式系统设计、DSP原理及应用、微机原理与应用、通信原理、语音信号处理等。
EDA Technology，Optics System Design，Optoelectronic Image Processing，Design of Embedded System，Principle and Application of DSP，Principles and Application of Micro-Computer，Principle and Technology of Optical Fiber Communication，Speech Signal Processing.

本科专业培养计划
Undergraduate Program for
Communication
Engineering Major
[2024级适用]
通信工程（080703）
大连海事大学教务处
2024年9月
通信工程专业本科培养计划
Undergraduate Program for Communication
Engineering Major
一、专业简介
I．Program Profile
大连海事大学通信工程专业始建于1958年船舶电气与导航专业，1984年正式命名为通信工程专业，是大连海事大学“211工程”及交通部“十五”和“十一五”规划重点建设专业。专业于2006年、2013年、2015年和2016年接连荣获辽宁省本科示范专业、省综合改革试点专业、省本科优势特色专业、省创新创业专业、省一流本科示范专业等称号，2013年位列辽宁省高校本科专业综合评价第一名。本专业主要培养具备通信系统和通信网络等方面的基础知识，能在通信领域从事通信系统、设备以及通信网络的研究、设计、制造、管理、应用和开发的高级工程技术人才。本专业是我校信息与通信工程一级学科硕士点和博士点的主要支撑专业。
本专业毕业生以理论扎实、适应能力强、国际视野开阔、综合素质高而获得用人单位的好评。除继续攻读硕士外，还可面向“互联网+”、移动通信网络、大数据、人工智能等领域就业，从事科研、技术开发、技术支持和管理工作。
Communication Engineering of Dalian Maritime University was founded in 1958，initially called Maritime Electrical and Navigation. In 1984, it was officially named as Communication Engineering, which is the key construction major of  “Project 211” in Dalian Maritime University, and the “Tenth Five-Year Plan” and the “Eleventh Five-Year Plan” of Ministry of Transport of the People's Republic of China. This major was successively awarded the titles of Liaoning Province Undergraduate Demonstration Major, Provincial Comprehensive Reform Pilot Major, Provincial Undergraduate Advantage Specialty, Provincial Innovation and Entrepreneurship Major, and Provincial First-class Undergraduate Demonstration Major in 2006, 2013, 2015 and 2016, respectively. In 2013, it ranked top 1 in the comprehensive evaluation of undergraduate majors of universities in Liaoning Province.
This major mainly cultivates senior engineering and technical personnel who have basic knowledge of communication systems and communication networks, and can engage in the research, design, manufacturing, management, application and development of communication systems, equipment and communication networks in the field of communication. This major is the main supporting one for the master's and doctoral programs of the first-level discipline of Information and Communication Engineering in Dalian Maritime University.
The graduates are well-recognized by employers for their solid theoretical background, strong adaptability, broad international vision, and high overall quality. In addition to pursuing a master's degree, the graduates can work in the fields of "Internet +", mobile communication networks, big data, artificial intelligence, etc., and engage in scientific research, technology development, technical support and management.
二、培养目标
II．Program Objectives
本专业致力于培养具有良好的科学素养和职业素养，能够在信息产业、交通运输、制造业、国防等行业的通信工程相关领域部门中，从事科学研究、设计开发、测试运维和服务管理等工作的复合型专业人才。
具体指标如下：
培养目标1：能够综合运用工程知识解决通信工程领域的工程问题，在工程问题解决过程中体现创新意识，并综合考虑社会、环境、法规、健康、安全与文化等因素影响；
培养目标2：在职业生涯中具有良好的人文社会科学素养、社会责任感和职业道德；
培养目标3：具备国际视野，具有沟通、交流与管理能力，在工作团队中，能作为主要成员发挥骨干作用；
培养目标4：具有自主学习和适应发展能力，具备终身学习意识。
This major aims to cultivate interdisciplinary professionals with good comprehensive qualities in humanities and social sciences, who can engage in scientific research, design and development, testing and maintenance, technical service and management in the field of communication engineering technology.
The students should be able to:
Have engineering knowledge to solve engineering problems in the field of communication engineering technology, with considering social, environmental, regulatory, health, safety and cultural factors, and with innovative consciousness in the process of solving engineering problems.
Have good humanities and Social Sciences literacy, social responsibility and professional ethics in their career;
Have international vision, communication and management skills, and being able to play a backbone role as a key member in a team.
Have the ability to learn independently and adapt to the development of society, and having the consciousness of lifelong learning.
三、毕业要求
III．Graduation Requirements
四、特色课程
IV．Feature Courses
5G无线传输技术、锁相与频率合成、现代数字交换原理、光纤通信、卫星通信、海上应急通信、移动通信、多媒体通信、现代电视原理。
5G Wireless Propagation Technology，Phase Lock & Frequency Synthesizer，Digital Switching Principles，Optical Fiber Communication，Satellite Communication，Digital Communication Theory and Applications，Multimedia Communication，Digital Microwave Communication，Principles of Modern Television.

1. 全校性选修课程分为人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程、创新与创业课程及其他课程。需要从人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程分别选修至少2学分，同时需要完成专业规定的任选课学分。具体课程见每年度选课系统中的全校选修课程一览。 The elective courses are divided into “humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”, “science and technology courses”, “innovation and entrepreneurship courses ”and “other courses”.  Among them, need to take at least 2 credits from “Humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”， “science and technology courses”， “innovation and entrepreneurship courses”, At the same time, it is necessary to complete the credits of elective courses specified by major.   2. 学生参加学校、院系组织的第二课堂活动，并符合学校有关学籍管理规定，可获得相应任选课学分，具体参考学生手册中的学籍管理规定部分。 If students participate in the second classroom activities organized by the school and departments, and meet the school's relevant regulations on student status management, they can obtain corresponding optional course credits. For details, please refer to the regulations on student status management in the student handbook.	1. 全校性选修课程分为人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程、创新与创业课程及其他课程。需要从人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程分别选修至少2学分，同时需要完成专业规定的任选课学分。具体课程见每年度选课系统中的全校选修课程一览。 The elective courses are divided into “humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”, “science and technology courses”, “innovation and entrepreneurship courses ”and “other courses”.  Among them, need to take at least 2 credits from “Humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”， “science and technology courses”， “innovation and entrepreneurship courses”, At the same time, it is necessary to complete the credits of elective courses specified by major.   2. 学生参加学校、院系组织的第二课堂活动，并符合学校有关学籍管理规定，可获得相应任选课学分，具体参考学生手册中的学籍管理规定部分。 If students participate in the second classroom activities organized by the school and departments, and meet the school's relevant regulations on student status management, they can obtain corresponding optional course credits. 1.全校性选修课程分为人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程、创新与创业课程及其他课程。需要从人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程分别选修至少2学分，同时需要完成专业规定的任选课学分。具体课程见每年度选课系统中的全校选修课程一览。 The elective courses are divided into “humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”, “science and technology courses”, “innovation and entrepreneurship courses ”and “other courses”.  Among them, Need to take at least 2 credits from “Humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”， “science and technology courses”, At the same time, it is necessary to complete the credits of elective courses specified by each major. For specific courses, please refer to the list of elective courses in the course selection system of each year.   2. 学生参加学校、院系组织的第二课堂活动，并符合学校有关学籍管理规定，可获得相应任选课学分，具体参考学生手册中的学籍管理规定部分。 If students participate in the second classroom activities organized by the school and departments, and meet the school's relevant regulations on student status management, they can obtain corresponding optional course credits. For details, please refer to the regulations on student status management in the student handbook.	1.全校性选修课程分为人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程、创新与创业课程及其他课程。需要从人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程分别选修至少2学分，同时需要完成专业规定的任选课学分。具体课程见每年度选课系统中的全校选修课程一览。 The elective courses are divided into “humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”, “science and technology courses”, “innovation and entrepreneurship courses ”and “other courses”.  Among them, Need to take at least 2 credits from “Humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”， “science and technology courses”, At the same time, it is necessary to complete the credits of elective courses specified by each major. 1. 全校性选修课程分为人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程、创新与创业课程及其他课程。需要从人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程分别选修至少2学分，同时需要完成专业规定的任选课学分。具体课程见每年度选课系统中的全校选修课程一览。 The elective courses are divided into “humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”, “science and technology courses”, “innovation and entrepreneurship courses ”and “other courses”.  Among them, need to take at least 2 credits from “Humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”， “science and technology courses”， “innovation and entrepreneurship courses”, At the same time, it is necessary to complete the credits of elective courses specified by major.   2. 学生参加学校、院系组织的第二课堂活动，并符合学校有关学籍管理规定，可获得相应任选课学分，具体参考学生手册中的学籍管理规定部分。 If students participate in the second classroom activities organized by the school and departments, and meet the school's relevant regulations on student status management, they can obtain corresponding optional course credits. For details, please refer to the regulations on student status management in the student handbook.	1. 全校性选修课程分为人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程、创新与创业课程及其他课程。需要从人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程分别选修至少2学分，同时需要完成专业规定的任选课学分。具体课程见每年度选课系统中的全校选修课程一览。 The elective courses are divided into “humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”, “science and technology courses”, “innovation and entrepreneurship courses ”and “other courses”.  Among them, need to take at least 2 credits from “Humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”， “science and technology courses”， “innovation and entrepreneurship courses”, At the same time, it is necessary to complete the credits of elective courses specified by major.   2. 学生参加学校、院系组织的第二课堂活动，并符合学校有关学籍管理规定，可获得相应任选课学分，具体参考学生手册中的学籍管理规定部分。 If students participate in the second classroom activities organized by the school and departments, and meet the school's relevant regulations on student status management, they can obtain corresponding optional course credits. 毕业要求1	工程知识：能够将数学、自然科学、工程基础知识、通信专业基础和专业知识，用于解决通信工程领域复杂工程问题。 Engineering knowledge: Be able to apply mathematics, natural sciences, basic knowledge of communication engineering, professional foundation and professional knowledge to solve complex communication engineering problems.
毕业要求2	问题分析：能够应用数学和工程科学的基本原理，识别、表达、并通过文献研究分析复杂通信工程问题，以获得有效结论。 Problem analysis: Apply the basic principles of mathematics and engineering science to identify, express and analyze complex communication engineering problems through literature research, in order to obtain effective conclusions.
毕业要求3	设计/开发解决方案：能够设计针对复杂通信工程问题的解决方案，设计满足特定需求的系统、模块、算法或流程，并能够在设计环节中体现创新意识，综合考虑社会、健康、安全、法律、文化及环境等因素。 Design/Development Solutions: Be able to design solutions to complex communication engineering problems, design systems, modules, algorithms or processes that meet specific needs, and embody innovation awareness in the design process, taking into account social, health, safety, legal, cultural and environmental factors.
毕业要求4	研究：能够基于科学原理并采用科学方法对复杂通信工程问题进行研究，包括设计实验、分析与解释数据，并通过信息综合得到合理有效的结论。 Research: Be able to study complex communication engineering problems based on scientific principles and using scientific methods, including designing experiments, analyzing and interpreting data, and obtaining reasonable and effective conclusions through information synthesis.
毕业要求5	使用现代工具：能够开发、选择与使用适当的技术、资源、现代工程工具和信息技术工具，对通信工程领域复杂工程问题进行预测与模拟；采集、整理和使用复杂工程问题相关信息数据；在现代工具使用过程中，理解其局限性。 Using modern tools: Be able to select, use and develop appropriate computer technology, resources, modern engineering tools and information technology tools for complex communication engineering problems, including prediction and Simulation of complex communication engineering problems, and to understand their limitations.
毕业要求6	工程与社会：能够基于通信工程相关背景知识进行合理分析，评价专业工程实践和复杂通信工程问题解决方案对社会、健康、安全、法律以及文化的影响，并理解应承担的责任。 Engineering and Society: Be able to conduct rational analysis based on the background knowledge of communication engineering, evaluate the impact of professional engineering practices and complex communication engineering problem solutions on society, health, safety, law and culture, and understand the responsibilities to be undertaken.
毕业要求7	环境和可持续发展：能够理解和评价复杂通信工程实践对环境、社会可持续发展的影响。 Environment and Sustainable Development: Be able to understand and evaluate the impact of complex communication engineering practices on the sustainable development of the environment and society.
毕业要求8	职业规范：具有人文社会科学素养和社会责任感，能够在通信工程实践中理解并遵守工程职业道德和规范，履行责任。 Professional norms: Have humanities and Social Sciences literacy and social responsibility, can understand and abide by engineering professional ethics and norms in communication engineering practice, and fulfill their responsibilities.
毕业要求9	个人和团队：能够适应多学科背景下的团队合作方式，并能在团队中承担个体、团队成员以及负责人的角色。 Individuals and teams: Be able to adapt to the Multi-disciplinary Background of team cooperation, and can assume the role of individuals, team members and leaders in the team.
毕业要求10	沟通：能够就复杂通信工程问题与业界同行及社会公众进行有效沟通，包括撰写报告和设计文稿、陈述发言、清晰表达或回应指令，并具备一定的国际视野，能够在跨文化背景下进行交流。 Communication: Be able to communicate effectively with colleagues in the industry and the public on complex communication engineering issues, including writing reports and designing manuscripts, presenting statements, clearly expressing or responding to instructions, with a certain international perspective, and able to communicate in a cross-cultural context.
毕业要求11	项目管理：理解并掌握工程管理原理与经济决策方法，并能在多学科环境中应用。 Project management: Understand and master the principles of engineering management and economic decision-making methods, and can be applied in a multidisciplinary environment.
毕业要求12	终身学习：具有自主学习和终身学习的意识，有不断学习和适应发展的能力。 Lifelong learning: Have the awareness of self-learning and lifelong learning, and the ability to constantly learn and adapt to development.

1. 全校性选修课程分为人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程、创新与创业课程及其他课程。需要从人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程分别选修至少2学分，同时需要完成专业规定的任选课学分。具体课程见每年度选课系统中的全校选修课程一览。 The elective courses are divided into “humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”, “science and technology courses”, “innovation and entrepreneurship courses ”and “other courses”.  Among them, need to take at least 2 credits from “Humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”， “science and technology courses”， “innovation and entrepreneurship courses”, At the same time, it is necessary to complete the credits of elective courses specified by major.    2. 学生参加学校、院系组织的第二课堂活动，并符合学校有关学籍管理规定，可获得相应任选课学分，具体参考学生手册中的学籍管理规定部分。 If students participate in the second classroom activities organized by the school and departments, and meet the school's relevant regulations on student status management, they can obtain corresponding optional course credits. For details, please refer to the regulations on student status management in the student handbook.	1. 全校性选修课程分为人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程、创新与创业课程及其他课程。需要从人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程分别选修至少2学分，同时需要完成专业规定的任选课学分。具体课程见每年度选课系统中的全校选修课程一览。 The elective courses are divided into “humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”, “science and technology courses”, “innovation and entrepreneurship courses ”and “other courses”.  Among them, need to take at least 2 credits from “Humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”， “science and technology courses”， “innovation and entrepreneurship courses”, At the same time, it is necessary to complete the credits of elective courses specified by major.    2. 学生参加学校、院系组织的第二课堂活动，并符合学校有关学籍管理规定，可获得相应任选课学分，具体参考学生手册中的学籍管理规定部分。 If students participate in the second classroom activities organized by the school and departments, and meet the school's relevant regulations on student status management, they can obtain corresponding optional course credits.
